Introduction

This documentation aims to provide all the information you need to work with our API.

As you scroll, you'll see code examples for working with the API in different programming languages in the dark area to the right (or as part of the content on mobile). You can switch the language used with the tabs at the top right (or from the nav menu at the top left on mobile).

Base URL

http://localhost

Authenticating requests

Authenticate requests to this API's endpoints by sending a query parameter apiKey in the request.

All authenticated endpoints are marked with a requires authentication badge in the documentation below.

You can retrieve your token by visiting your dashboard and clicking Generate API token.

Auth

APIs for Auth users

Create User

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://localhost/api/v1/auth/register" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \

Request      

POST api/v1/auth/register

Body Parameters

user_name   string   

email   string   

Must be a valid email address.

password   string   

Must be at least 8 characters.

first_name   string   

last_name   string   

phone   string  optional  

country   string  optional  

status   string  optional  

Must be one of married, single, or engaged.

region   string  optional  

birthday   string  optional  

Must be a valid date.

gender   string  optional  

Must be one of male or female.

Login The User

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://localhost/api/v1/auth/login" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"email\": \"lula.goodwin@example.com\",
    \"password\": \"culpa\"
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost/api/v1/auth/login"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "email": "lula.goodwin@example.com",
    "password": "culpa"
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());
Received response:
Request failed with error:

Request      

POST api/v1/auth/login

Body Parameters

email   string   

Must be a valid email address.

password   string   

Logout User

requires authentication

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://localhost/api/v1/auth/logout?apiKey=%7BYOUR_AUTH_KEY%7D" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost/api/v1/auth/logout"
);

const params = {
    "apiKey": "{YOUR_AUTH_KEY}",
};
Object.keys(params)
    .forEach(key => url.searchParams.append(key, params[key]));

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
Received response:
Request failed with error:

Request      

POST api/v1/auth/logout

Query Parameters

apiKey   string   

Authentication key.

Comment

APIs for comment on post

comments for one post

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://localhost/api/v1/comments/post/1" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost/api/v1/comments/post/1"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());

PUT api/v1/comments/{comment_id}

URL Parameters

comment_id   integer   

The ID of the comment.

Query Parameters

apiKey   string   

Authentication key.

Body Parameters

body   string  optional  

This field is required when photos is not present.

photos   string[]  optional  

This field is required when body is not present. Must not be greater than 10000 characters.

delete Comment

requires authentication

Deleting a comment is by the owner of the comment or post.😕
Example request:
curl --request DELETE \
    "http://localhost/api/v1/comments/1?apiKey=%7BYOUR_AUTH_KEY%7D" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost/api/v1/comments/1"
);

const params = {
    "apiKey": "{YOUR_AUTH_KEY}",
};
Object.keys(params)
    .forEach(key => url.searchParams.append(key, params[key]));

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "DELETE",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
Received response:
Request failed with error:

);

};

update post

requires authentication

const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost/api/v1/posts/1"
);

const params = {
    "apiKey": "{YOUR_AUTH_KEY}",
};
Object.keys(params)
    .forEach(key => url.searchParams.append(key, params[key]));

    "Accept": "application/json",
};

    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost/api/v1/profiles/1/images"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
